39 #define SPLASH_IMAGE_RUN_LENGTH_DECODE(image_buf, rle_data, size, bpp) do \
40 { unsigned int __bpp; unsigned char *__ip; const unsigned char *__il, *__rd; \
41  __bpp = (bpp); __ip = (image_buf); __il = __ip + (size) * __bpp; \
42  __rd = (rle_data); if (__bpp > 3) { /* RGBA */ \
43  while (__ip < __il) { unsigned int __l = *(__rd++); \
44  if (__l & 128) { __l = __l - 128; \
45  do { memcpy (__ip, __rd, 4); __ip += 4; } while (--__l); __rd += 4; \
46  } else { __l *= 4; memcpy (__ip, __rd, __l); \
47  __ip += __l; __rd += __l; } } \
48  } else if (__bpp == 3) { /* RGB */ \
49  while (__ip < __il) { unsigned int __l = *(__rd++); \
50  if (__l & 128) { __l = __l - 128; \
51  do { memcpy (__ip, __rd, 3); __ip += 3; } while (--__l); __rd += 3; \
52  } else { __l *= 3; memcpy (__ip, __rd, __l); \
53  __ip += __l; __rd += __l; } } \
54  } else { /* RGB16 */ \
55  while (__ip < __il) { unsigned int __l = *(__rd++); \
56  if (__l & 128) { __l = __l - 128; \
57  do { memcpy (__ip, __rd, 2); __ip += 2; } while (--__l); __rd += 2; \
58  } else { __l *= 2; memcpy (__ip, __rd, __l); \
59  __ip += __l; __rd += __l; } } \
60  } } while (0)
61
